\section{Project Concept (Complete Overview)}
This project implements a complete real-time 3D Solar System simulation using C++ and Modern OpenGL (core profile).
The architecture combines simulation logic, GPU rendering, matrix-based transformations, texture mapping, camera interaction, and classic graphics algorithms.

\subsection{High-Level Pipeline}
The execution flow is: initialize window and OpenGL state; load shaders/meshes/textures; update planet states each frame using delta time; render skybox, sun, planets, rings, and helper visuals.

\subsection{Core Graphics Concepts Used}
\begin{itemize}
\item Primitive drawing with points, line loops, and triangle meshes.
\item 3D camera view/projection transformations for interactive navigation.
\item Lighting and material parameters through shader uniforms.
\item Texture mapping for realistic planet surfaces and environment background.
\item Transformation composition: translation, rotation, scaling, reflection, and shear.
\item Classical algorithms integrated into rendering helpers: Midpoint Circle, DDA, and Bresenham.
\end{itemize}

\subsection{File Coverage Note}
This document explains all project-authored files from root, include, src, and shaders directories.
Auto-generated build outputs and third-party vendor code are excluded because they are not authored project logic.
